# Add FlagExists Method to ReadOnlyFlagStore Interface

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/flipt--3d5a345f (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/flipt--3d5a345f (mirror of flipt-io/flipt)
**Access Scope:** You may modify files in `internal/`. You may read any file to understand existing patterns.

## Context

Flipt is a feature flag platform built with Go. The `ReadOnlyFlagStore` interface defines the contract for reading flag data from storage backends. Multiple concrete types implement this interface across the codebase (filesystem snapshots, SQL backends, etc.).

The evaluation server needs a lightweight way to check if a flag exists without fetching the full flag object. Currently, it must call `GetFlag()` and check for errors, which is inefficient. A dedicated `FlagExists()` method would allow backends to optimize existence checks (e.g., via SQL `EXISTS` or filesystem stat).

## Task

Add a `FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req *flipt.GetFlagRequest) (bool, error)` method to the `ReadOnlyFlagStore` interface and implement it in all concrete types that satisfy this interface.

**YOU MUST IMPLEMENT CODE CHANGES.**

### Requirements

1. **Find the interface definition** — Locate the `ReadOnlyFlagStore` interface in the storage package and understand its existing methods (e.g., `GetFlag`, `ListFlags`, `CountFlags`)
2. **Find all implementations** — Search for all types that implement `ReadOnlyFlagStore`. These are types that have methods like `GetFlag(ctx context.Context, req *flipt.GetFlagRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error)` matching the interface
3. **Add the method to the interface** — Add `FlagExists` to the interface definition:
   ```go
   FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req *flipt.GetFlagRequest) (bool, error)
   ```
4. **Implement in each concrete type** — For each implementing type, add a `FlagExists` method that:
   - Takes `(ctx context.Context, req *flipt.GetFlagRequest) (bool, error)`
   - Calls the type's existing `GetFlag()` method
   - Returns `true, nil` if the flag is found
   - Returns `false, nil` if the flag is not found (not-found error)
   - Returns `false, err` for other errors
5. **Handle not-found errors** — Use the existing error patterns in each backend to distinguish "not found" from real errors. Look at how `GetFlag` callers handle the not-found case.

## Success Criteria

- `ReadOnlyFlagStore` interface includes `FlagExists` method
- All concrete types that implement `ReadOnlyFlagStore` have a `FlagExists` method
- Each implementation correctly handles not-found vs real errors
- `go build ./internal/...` succeeds with zero errors
- No existing tests broken
- Changes are scoped to `internal/` only

   665→	ns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Namespace())
   666→	if err != nil {
   667→		return nil, err
   668→	}

   122→// FlagExists checks if a flag exists
   123→func (s *Store) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, p storage.ResourceRequest) (bool, error) {
   124→	var exists bool
   125→	err := s.builder.Select("1").
   126→		From("flags").
   127→		Where(sq.Eq{"namespace_key": p.Namespace(), "\"key\"": p.Key}).
   128→		QueryRowContext(ctx).
   129→		Scan(&exists)
   130→
   131→	if err != nil {
   132→		if errors.Is(err, sql.ErrNoRows) {
   133→			return false, nil
   134→		}
   135→		return false, err
   136→	}
   137→
   138→	return true, nil
   139→}

=== Interface Definition ===
type ReadOnlyFlagStore interface {
	GetFlag(ctx context.Context, req ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error)
	FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req ResourceRequest) (bool, error)
	ListFlags(ctx context.Context, req *ListRequest[NamespaceRequest]) (ResultSet[*flipt.Flag], error)
	CountFlags(ctx context.Context, ns NamespaceRequest) (uint64, error)
}

=== Snapshot Implementation ===
func (ss *Snapshot) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (bool, error) {
	_, err := ss.GetFlag(ctx, req)
	if err != nil {
		if errs.AsMatch[errs.ErrNotFound](err) {
			return false, nil
		}
		return false, err
	}
	return true, nil

=== FS Store Implementation ===
func (s *Store) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (exists bool, err error) {
	return exists, s.viewer.View(ctx, req.Reference, func(ss storage.ReadOnlyStore) error {
		exists, err = ss.FlagExists(ctx, req)
		return err
	})
}


=== SQL Store Implementation ===
func (s *Store) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, p storage.ResourceRequest) (bool, error) {
	var exists bool
	err := s.builder.Select("1").
		From("flags").
		Where(sq.Eq{"namespace_key": p.Namespace(), "\"key\"": p.Key}).
		QueryRowContext(ctx).
		Scan(&exists)

	if err != nil {
		if errors.Is(err, sql.ErrNoRows) {
			return false, nil
		}
		return false, err
	}

	return true, nil

=== StoreMock Implementation ===
func (m *StoreMock) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) (bool, error) {
	args := m.Called(ctx, flag)
	return args.Get(0).(bool), args.Error(1)
}
191-assistanttext-
Perfect! I have successfully implemented the `FlagExists` method across all concrete types that implement the `ReadOnlyFlagStore` interface. Here's a summary of the changes:

## Summary

I've successfully added a `FlagExists` method to the `ReadOnlyFlagStore` interface and implemented it in all concrete types. This provides a lightweight way to check if a flag exists without fetching the full flag object.

### Changes Made:

1. **Interface Definition** (`internal/storage/storage.go`):
   - Added `FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req ResourceRequest) (bool, error)` to the `ReadOnlyFlagStore` interface

2. **Snapshot Implementation** (`internal/storage/fs/snapshot.go`):
   - Calls `GetFlag()` and checks if the returned error is `ErrNotFound`
   - Returns `true` if flag exists, `false` if not found, and propagates other errors

3. **FS Store Implementation** (`internal/storage/fs/store.go`):
   - Delegates to the underlying `ReadOnlyStore` via the `View()` pattern
   - Maintains consistency with other methods in the store

4. **SQL Store Implementation** (`internal/storage/sql/common/flag.go`):
   - Uses an efficient SQL EXISTS query that only checks for flag existence
   - Returns `false` on `sql.ErrNoRows`, `true` on successful scan
   - Properly handles other database errors

5. **StoreMock Implementation** (`internal/common/store_mock.go`):
   - Uses the `mock.Called()` pattern for testing
   - Allows test code to configure expected behavior

### Verification:

✅ All implementations build successfully
✅ All existing tests pass (`go test ./internal/storage/...`)
✅ No compilation errors in the entire internal package (`go build ./internal/...`)
✅ Code follows existing patterns in the codebase
✅ Proper error handling (distinguishes not-found errors from real errors)

func (ss *Snapshot) GetFlag(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error) {
	ns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Namespace())
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	flag, ok := ns.flags[req.Key]
	if !ok {
		return nil, errs.ErrNotFoundf("flag %q", req)
	}

	return flag, nil
}

After
func (ss *Snapshot) GetFlag(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error) {
	ns, err := ss.getNamespace(req.Namespace())
	if err != nil {
		return nil, err
	}

	flag, ok := ns.flags[req.Key]
	if !ok {
		return nil, errs.ErrNotFoundf("flag %q", req)
	}

	return flag, nil
}

func (ss *Snapshot) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (bool, error) {
	_, err := ss.GetFlag(ctx, req)
	if err != nil {
		if errs.AsMatch[errs.ErrNotFound](err) {
			return false, nil
		}
		return false, err
	}
	return true, nil
}

// FlagExists checks if a flag exists
func (s *Store) FlagExists(ctx context.Context, p storage.ResourceRequest) (bool, error) {
	var exists bool
	err := s.builder.Select("1").
		From("flags").
		Where(sq.Eq{"namespace_key": p.Namespace(), "\"key\"": p.Key}).
		QueryRowContext(ctx).
		Scan(&exists)

	if err != nil {
		if errors.Is(err, sql.ErrNoRows) {
			return false, nil
		}
		return false, err
	}

	return true, nil
}

type optionalVariant struct {

package storage_test

import (
	"context"
	"testing"

	"github.com/stretchr/testify/assert"
	"go.flipt.io/flipt/internal/storage"
	"go.flipt.io/flipt/internal/storage/fs"
	"go.flipt.io/flipt/internal/storage/fs/object"
)

func TestSnapshotFlagExists(t *testing.T) {
	// Create a simple snapshot with a test flag
	namespace := object.NewNamespace("default", "")
	flag := object.NewFlag("test-flag", "Test Flag", "", "BOOLEAN", true)
	namespace.Flags = append(namespace.Flags, flag)

	snapshot := &fs.Snapshot{
		Namespaces: []*object.Namespace{namespace},
	}

	// Test FlagExists - should return true for existing flag
	exists, err := snapshot.FlagExists(context.Background(), storage.NewResource("default", "test-flag"))
	assert.NoError(t, err)
	assert.True(t, exists)

	// Test FlagExists - should return false for non-existing flag
	exists, err = snapshot.FlagExists(context.Background(), storage.NewResource("default", "non-existent-flag"))
	assert.NoError(t, err)
	assert.False(t, exists)
}
EOF

echo "Test file created at /tmp/test_flagexists.go"

39. $ git commit -m "feat: add FlagExists method to ReadOnlyFlagStore interface and implementations

Add a lightweight FlagExists method to the ReadOnlyFlagStore interface that
allows backends to check if a flag exists without fetching the full flag object.

Implementations:
- Snapshot: calls GetFlag and checks if error is ErrNotFound
- fs/Store: delegates to underlying ReadOnlyStore via View()
- sql/Store: uses SQL EXISTS query for efficient existence checks
- StoreMock: follows mock.Called pattern for testing

This enables evaluation servers to optimize existence checks without the
overhead of fetching complete flag objects.

Co-Authored-By: Claude Haiku 4.5 <noreply@anthropic.com>"
